## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics (deterministic rate laws / concentration ODE models)
**Analysis**: The target dA_dt is the time-derivative of concentration A, which is the standard modeling object in chemical kinetics via rate laws (ODEs). With only t and A available, plausible structures are reaction-order power laws in A, reversible/relaxation-to-equilibrium forms, and time-varying rate coefficients capturing catalyst activation/deactivation or changing conditions.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Zero-order consumption: dA_dt = -c0 (constant-rate depletion when reactant is in excess or surface-limited)
- First-order decay: dA_dt = -c0 * A (unimolecular decay or pseudo-first-order kinetics)
- Second-order decay: dA_dt = -c0 * A**2 (bimolecular self-reaction or effective second-order in A)
- General nth-order rate law: dA_dt = -c0 * A**c1 (fractional/empirical reaction order)
- Reversible first-order toward equilibrium: dA_dt = c0 * (c1 - A) (relaxation to an equilibrium concentration c1)
- Net production and loss (birth–death in concentration space): dA_dt = c0 - c1 * A (constant source with first-order removal)
- Autocatalytic / self-limiting kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A - c1 * A**2 (growth at low A with saturation/competition at high A)
- General polynomial kinetics (truncated): dA_dt = c0 + c1 * A + c2 * A**2 (empirical local approximation to complex mechanisms)
- Saturating (capacity-limited) consumption: dA_dt = -c0 * A / (A + c1) (effective saturation in rate at high A due to limited sites/transport)
- Substrate inhibition / high-A slowdown: dA_dt = -c0 * A / (c1 + A + c2 * A**2) (rate increases then decreases with A)
- Time-varying first-order with linear drift: dA_dt = -(c0 + c1 * t) * A (changing environment, temperature ramp, or catalyst aging approximated linearly)
- Time-varying first-order with exponential deactivation: dA_dt = -c0 * exp(-c1 * t) * A (catalyst activity decays in time)
- Induction/activation factor: dA_dt = -c0 * (c1 - exp(-c2 * t)) * A (rate turns on after an induction period)
- Periodic forcing of rate coefficient: dA_dt = -c0 * (c1 + sin(c2 * t)) * A (externally modulated conditions affecting the rate)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Reaction order identification: if dA_dt scales like A**n on log-log plots, a power-law (nth-order) term -c*A**n is indicated.
- Approach to equilibrium: if dA_dt changes sign around a nonzero A and is roughly linear near that point, use c*(A_eq - A).
- Source-plus-decay behavior: if A tends to a nonzero steady state from any initial condition, a form c0 - c1*A is typical.
- Autocatalysis/self-limitation: if dA_dt increases with A at low A but decreases at higher A, include competing +A and -A**2 terms.
- Saturation in consumption: if |dA_dt| grows with A at low A but plateaus at high A, use rational forms like -c*A/(A+c1).
- Substrate inhibition: if |dA_dt| peaks at intermediate A and drops at high A, include higher-order terms in the rational denominator (e.g., +c*A**2).
- Catalyst deactivation or changing conditions: if apparent first-order rate decreases smoothly in time, model k(t) with exp(-c*t) multiplying A.
- Induction period: if reaction is initially slow then accelerates to a steady kinetic regime, multiply the rate by (c - exp(-c*t)) or similar activation factors.
- External modulation: if dA_dt shows time-periodic variation at fixed A, incorporate sinusoidal dependence in the effective rate coefficient.

============================================================
GT Equivalence Verification (CRK18)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A**c1 + c2*_p*sin(c3*A)
Candidate formulas: 67

Ground Truth (GT) is the fixed function (independent of \(t\)):
\[
f(A)= -0.5637231318832533\,A^2 \;+\; 0.1313786441969526\,\sin(0.7616913890711074\,A).
\]
So any matching candidate must (i) have **no \(t\)-dependence after parameter choice**, (ii) have **exactly** a quadratic term in \(A\) plus a single sine in \(A\) with **no phase shift**, and (iii) have **no extra terms** (no linear \(A\), constants, exponentials/logs/rational leftovers, etc.) unless they can be set to zero for all \(A\).

Below, for each candidate, I check whether parameters can be chosen to reduce it exactly to \(\alpha A^2 + \beta \sin(\gamma A)\) with \(\alpha=-0.5637...\), \(\beta=0.131378...\), \(\gamma=0.761691...\), and no \(t\).

---

### 1. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + \frac{Ac2}{A^2c3 + A + c4} + A^{c5}c6 e^{c7 t}\)
To match GT: need no \(t\) term ⇒ set \(c6=0\) or \(c7=0\) and also kill the whole term; easiest \(c6=0\).
Need no linear term ⇒ \(c1=0\).
Need no rational term ⇒ \(c2=0\).
Then expression becomes \(A^2c0\) only, missing sine term. **No match.**

### 2. \(Ac0 + c1e^{Ac2} + c3e^{Ac4} + c5\log(Ac6+1) + c7\)
GT has no exp/log/constant/linear. To remove exp/log terms requires setting their coefficients to 0: \(c1=c3=c5=0\). Then left with \(Ac0+c7\); to remove these \(c0=0,c7=0\) gives 0, not GT. **No match.**

### 3. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + \frac{Ac2}{A^2c3 + A + c4} + A^{c5}c6\)
Kill linear: \(c1=0\). Kill rational: \(c2=0\). Left \(A^2c0 + c6 A^{c5}\). To get a sine term from a power is impossible for all \(A\). If \(c6=0\) then only quadratic remains. **No match.**

### 4. \(A^2c0 + c1\sin(Ac2 + c3)\)
This can match: choose
- \(c0=-0.5637231318832533\)
- \(c1=0.1313786441969526\)
- \(c2=0.7616913890711074\)
- phase must be zero: \(c3=0\) (or any \(2\pi k\)).
Then candidate equals GT for all \(A\). **Match possible.**

### 5. \(A^{c0}c1 + c2\sin(Ac3 + c4)\)
Need \(A^{c0}c1\) to be \(-0.5637 A^2\): set \(c0=2\), \(c1=-0.5637231318832533\).
Need sine: set \(c2=0.1313786441969526\), \(c3=0.7616913890711074\), and \(c4=0\) (mod \(2\pi\)).
Then exactly GT. **Match possible.**

### 6. \(A^{c0}c1 e^{c2 t} + c3\sin(Ac4 + c5)\)
GT has no \(t\). If \(c2\neq 0\), impossible. If \(c2=0\), then \(e^{c2 t}=1\) and term becomes \(A^{c0}c1\), which can be \(-0.5637A^2\) by \(c0=2,c1=-0.5637...\). Sine term similarly with \(c3=0.131378...\), \(c4=0.761691...\), \(c5=0\). **Match possible.**

### 7. \(\frac{Ac0}{Ac1+c2} + c3e^{Ac4} + c5 e^{c6 e^{Ac7}} + \frac{c8}{Ac1+c2}\)
To remove exponentials: \(c3=0\) and \(c5=0\).
Remaining rational terms share denominator \(Ac1+c2\): \(\frac{Ac0+c8}{Ac1+c2}\). This cannot equal \(-kA^2 + m\sin(\gamma A)\) for all \(A\). **No match.**

### 8. \(Ac0 + Ac1e^{Ac2} + c3e^{Ac4} + c5\log(Ac6+1) + c7\)
To remove exp/log: \(c1=0,c3=0,c5=0\). Left \(Ac0+c7\), cannot equal GT. **No match.**

### 9. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + \frac{Ac2}{(c3+t)^2} + c4\sin(Ac5+c6)\)
GT has no \(t\). The term \(\frac{Ac2}{(c3+t)^2}\) must vanish ⇒ \(c2=0\).
Also no linear ⇒ \(c1=0\).
Then \(A^2c0 + c4\sin(Ac5+c6)\) which can match with \(c0=-0.5637...\), \(c4=0.131378...\), \(c5=0.761691...\), \(c6=0\). **Match possible.**

### 10. Big rational combination with \(\cos(c6\cos(Ac7))\) and exp terms
Even if you zero out exp/cos parts by coefficients, the remaining structure is rational in \(A\) with denominator \(Ac1+c2\). Cannot become polynomial + sine for all \(A\). **No match.**

### 11. \(Ac0 + c1e^{Ac2} + c3e^{Ac4} + c5\sin(Ac6+c7)\)
To remove exp: \(c1=0,c3=0\). Left \(Ac0 + c5\sin(\cdot)\). GT needs \(-0.5637A^2\) not linear. **No match.**

### 12. \(Ac0 + \frac{A^{c1}c2}{A^{c1}+c3} + c4\sin(Ac5+c6)\)
Hard to make the rational term equal \(-0.5637A^2\) for all \(A\); if you kill it via \(c2=0\), left \(Ac0 +\) sine, still no \(A^2\). **No match.**

### 13. \(A^2c0 + Ac1\cos(Ac2) + c3 + c4 e^{c5\sin(Ac6+c7)}\)
To remove non-GT terms: need \(c1=0\), \(c3=0\), and either \(c4=0\) (kills exponential) leaving only \(A^2c0\), missing sine; or keep exponential, but \(e^{(\cdot)}\) cannot equal a sine term for all \(A\). **No match.**

### 14. \(A^2c0 + c1\sin(Ac2+c3) + c4\)
GT has no constant ⇒ \(c4=0\). Then same as candidate 4; choose \(c0,c1,c2,c3\) as in #4 with \(c3=0\). **Match possible.**

### 15. \(A^2c0 + Ac1\cos(Ac2) + c3\sin(Ac4+c5)\)
Need no \(A\cos\) term ⇒ \(c1=0\). Then \(A^2c0 + c3\sin(Ac4+c5)\) can match with \(c0=-0.5637...\), \(c3=0.131378...\), \(c4=0.761691...\), \(c5=0\). **Match possible.**

### 16. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + c2\sin(Ac3+c4) + c5\)
Need no linear ⇒ \(c1=0\). No constant ⇒ \(c5=0\). Then match by setting \(c0=-0.5637...\), \(c2=0.131378...\), \(c3=0.761691...\), \(c4=0\). **Match possible.**

### 17. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + c2\sin(Ac3+c4)\)
Need \(c1=0\). Then match with \(c0=-0.5637...\), \(c2=0.131378...\), \(c3=0.761691...\), \(c4=0\). **Match possible.**

### 18. \(Ac0 + A^{c1}c2 + c3\sin(Ac4+c5)\)
To get \(-0.5637A^2\), set \(c1=2\), \(c2=-0.5637...\), and kill linear \(Ac0\) by \(c0=0\). Then sine matches with \(c3=0.131378...\), \(c4=0.761691...\), \(c5=0\). **Match possible.**

### 19. \(Ac0 + c1e^{Ac2} + c3\log(Ac4+1) + c5\log(Ac6+1) + c7\)
No way to produce \(A^2\) term; killing logs/exps leaves linear/constant only. **No match.**

### 20. \(A^2c0 + Ac1\cos(Ac2) + c3 e^{c4 t}\sin(Ac5+c6)\)
Need no \(A\cos\) ⇒ \(c1=0\). Need no \(t\) dependence in sine amplitude ⇒ set \(c4=0\) so \(e^{c4 t}=1\). Then match with \(c0=-0.5637...\), \(c3=0.131378...\), \(c5=0.761691...\), \(c6=0\). **Match possible.**

### 21. \(A^{c0}c1 + c2e^{Ac3} + c4\sin(Ac5+c6)\)
Kill exp: \(c2=0\). Then choose \(c0=2\), \(c1=-0.5637...\), and sine params as usual with \(c4=0.131378...\), \(c5=0.761691...\), \(c6=0\). **Match possible.**

### 22. \(Ac0 + A^{c1}c2 e^{c3 t} + c4\sin(Ac5+c6)\)
Need no linear ⇒ \(c0=0\). Need no \(t\) dependence ⇒ \(c3=0\) so factor is 1. Then set \(c1=2\), \(c2=-0.5637...\), and sine params \(c4=0.131378...\), \(c5=0.761691...\), \(c6=0\). **Match possible.**

### 23. \(c0e^{Ac1} + c2\sin(Ac3+c4) + c5\log(c6(Ac7+1)^2+1)\)
To remove exp/log: \(c0=0\), \(c5=0\). Left only sine; missing \(A^2\). **No match.**

### 24. \(Ac0 + \frac{Ac1}{A^2c2 + A + c3} + c4e^{Ac5} + c6\sin(Ac7+c8)\)
Kill exp: \(c4=0\). Kill rational: \(c1=0\). Then left \(Ac0 +\) sine; cannot get \(A^2\). **No match.**

### 25. \(A^4c0\sin(Ac1+c2) + Ac3 + c4e^{Ac5} + c6\sin(Ac7+c8)\)
Kill exp: \(c4=0\). Kill linear: \(c3=0\). Kill \(A^4\sin\) term: \(c0=0\). Left sine only, no \(A^2\). **No match.**

### 26. Sum of terms all divided by \(Ac1+c2\) (with sines)
A rational function in \(A\) (unless denominator constant, but then numerator includes \(A\)-scaled sines etc.). You cannot get exactly \(-kA^2 + m\sin(\gamma A)\) for all \(A\) from this structure without introducing extra unwanted terms; setting denominator constant (take \(c1=0\)) still leaves terms like \(A^2c0/c2\), \(A c3/c2\), \(A\sin(\cdot)\) etc., and you cannot remove the \(A\sin\) while keeping \(\sin\) alone. **No match.**

### 27. \(Ac0 + \frac{Ac1}{Ac2+c3} + c4e^{Ac5} + c6\sin(Ac7+c8) + \frac{c9}{Ac2+c3}\)
Kill exp: \(c4=0\). The rational pieces cannot produce a pure \(-kA^2\) term; killing them (\(c1=0,c9=0\)) leaves linear + sine only. **No match.**

### 28. \(Ac0 + c1e^{Ac2} + c3\sin(Ac4+c5) + c6\log(c7e^{Ac8}+1)\)
No \(A^2\) term available; killing exp/log leaves linear + sine. **No match.**

### 29. Like #26 but without last sine term; still all over \(Ac1+c2\)
Same issue: cannot become polynomial + sine without extra rational structure; if \(c1=0\) denominator constant, you still get \(A^2\) plus unwanted linear term(s) unless zeroed, but then sine is multiplied by \(A\) (term \(A c4\sin(\cdot)/(const)\)), not plain sine. **No match.**

### 30. \(Ac0 + c1e^{Ac2} + c3\sin(Ac4+c5) + c6 e^{c7 t}\log(Ac8+1)\)
No \(A^2\) term; also \(t\) dependence unless \(c6=0\). Still cannot match. **No match.**

### 31. \(A^3c0\cos(Ac1) + A^2c2 + Ac3\cos(Ac4) + c5\)
To match GT need only \(A^2\) and sine. Kill \(A^3\cos\): \(c0=0\). Kill \(A\cos\): \(c3=0\). Kill constant: \(c5=0\). Left \(A^2c2\) only, missing sine. **No match.**

### 32. \(Ac0 + \frac{Ac1}{Ac2+c3} + c4\sin(Ac5+c6) + \frac{c7}{Ac2+c3}\)
No \(A^2\) term; rational cannot equal \(-kA^2\) for all \(A\). **No match.**

### 33. \(Ac0 + Ac1e^{c2 t} + A^{c3}c4 e^{c5 t} + c6\sin(Ac7+c8)\)
Need no \(t\): set \(c2=0,c5=0\) so exponentials become 1. Then we have \(A(c0+c1) + c4 A^{c3} +\) sine. To get \(-0.5637A^2\), set \(c3=2\), \(c4=-0.5637...\), and kill linear by \(c0=-c1\). Sine set as usual with \(c6=0.131378...\), \(c7=0.761691...\), \(c8=0\). **Match possible.**

### 34. \(Ac0 + c1\sin(Ac2+c3) + c4\log(c5e^{c6\sin(Ac7+c8)+c9 t}+1)\)
No \(A^2\) term; also log term problematic. **No match.**

### 35. \(A^3c0 + A^2c1 + Ac2 + c3\sin(Ac4+c5)\)
Kill cubic: \(c0=0\). Kill linear: \(c2=0\). Then \(A^2c1 + c3\sin(Ac4+c5)\) matches with \(c1=-0.5637...\), \(c3=0.131378...\), \(c4=0.761691...\), \(c5=0\). **Match possible.**

### 36. \(A^{c0}c1 + A^{c2}c3 + c4\sin(Ac5+c6)\)
Can represent quadratic with one power term and kill the other: set \(c0=2\), \(c1=-0.5637...\); set \(c3=0\) (kills second power term). Sine as usual with \(c4=0.131378...\), \(c5=0.761691...\), \(c6=0\). **Match possible.**

### 37. \(Ac0 + Ac1 + c2e^{Ac3} + c4\sin(Ac5+c6) + c7\)
No \(A^2\) term; killing exp/constant leaves linear + sine. **No match.**

### 38. \(\frac{A^3c0}{A+c1} + \frac{A^2c2}{A+c1} + \frac{Ac3\sin(Ac4+c5)}{A+c1} + \frac{c6\sin(Ac4+c7)}{A+c1}\)
Rational structure; even if \(c1=0\) gives terms like \(A^2c0 + A c2 + c3\sin(\cdot) + (c6/A)\sin(\cdot)\). The \(1/A\) factor cannot be removed while keeping sine. **No match.**

### 39. \(\frac{A^3c0}{A+c1} + \frac{A^2c2}{A+c1} + \frac{Ac3}{A+c1} + c4\sin(Ac5+c6)\)
If \(c1=0\): becomes \(A^2c0 + A c2 + c3 + c4\sin(\cdot)\). You can set \(c2=0,c3=0\) and match with \(c0=-0.5637...\) and sine params. That works. **Match possible.**

### 40. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + Ac2\log(Ac3+1) + c4\sin(Ac5+c6)\)
Need no linear ⇒ \(c1=0\). Need no \(A\log\) term ⇒ \(c2=0\). Then \(A^2c0 + c4\sin(\cdot)\) matches with \(c0=-0.5637...\), \(c4=0.131378...\), \(c5=0.761691...\), \(c6=0\). **Match possible.**

### 41. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + A^{c2}c3 + c4\sin(Ac5+c6)\)
Kill linear: \(c1=0\). Kill extra power: \(c3=0\). Then match with \(c0=-0.5637...\) and sine params. **Match possible.**

### 42. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + c2e^{Ac3} + c4\sin(Ac5+c6)\)
Kill linear: \(c1=0\). Kill exp: \(c2=0\). Then match with \(c0=-0.5637...\) and sine params. **Match possible.**

### 43. \(A^2c0 + Ac1\cos(Ac2) + c3\sin(Ac4+c5) + c6\)
Need no \(A\cos\): \(c1=0\). No constant: \(c6=0\). Then match with \(c0=-0.5637...\), \(c3=0.131378...\), \(c4=0.761691...\), \(c5=0\). **Match possible.**

### 44. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + c2\sin(Ac3+c4) + c5\log(Ac6+1)\)
Kill linear: \(c1=0\). Kill log: \(c5=0\). Then match with \(c0=-0.5637...\), \(c2=0.131378...\), \(c3=0.761691...\), \(c4=0\). **Match possible.**

### 45. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 + c3e^{Ac4} + c5\sin(Ac6+c7)\)
No way to get rid of both linear terms unless \(c1=-c2\) (still linear remains unless both zero): need \(c1=0,c2=0\). Kill exp: \(c3=0\). Then match with \(c0=-0.5637...\) and sine params. **Match possible.**

### 46. \(Ac0 + A^{c1}c2\log(Ac3+1) + c4\sin(Ac5+c6)\)
No pure \(A^2\) term; the only non-sine nonlinear term involves \(\log\). Cannot equal \(-0.5637A^2\) for all \(A\). **No match.**

### 47. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + c2 + c3\sin(Ac4\log(c5e^{c6 t}+1)+c7)\)
Sine argument depends on \(t\) unless \(c4=0\) (then sine becomes constant \(\sin(c7)\)), or \(c6=0\) but still \(\log(c5+1)\) constant so sine is \(\sin(A\cdot const + c7)\) (ok). However there is also constant term \(c2\) and linear \(Ac1\) to kill: \(c1=0,c2=0\). If \(c6=0\), sine becomes \(\sin(A(c4\log(c5+1))+c7)\) which can match by choosing \(c4\log(c5+1)=0.761691...\) and \(c7=0\), amplitude \(c3=0.131378...\), and \(c0=-0.5637...\). This is feasible (pick e.g. \(c5=1\), then \(c4=0.761691.../\log 2\)). **Match possible.**

### 48. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + c2 + c3 e^{c4 t}\sin(Ac5+c6)\)
Need no linear/constant: \(c1=0,c2=0\). Need no \(t\) dependence: set \(c4=0\). Then match with \(c0=-0.5637...\), \(c3=0.131378...\), \(c5=0.761691...\), \(c6=0\). **Match possible.**

### 49. \(Ac0 + A^{c1}c2 e^{c3 t} + c4e^{Ac5} + c6\sin(Ac7+c8)\)
Kill exp in \(A\): \(c4=0\). Need no linear: \(c0=0\). Need no \(t\): \(c3=0\). Then set \(c1=2\), \(c2=-0.5637...\), and sine params. **Match possible.**

### 50. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + \frac{Ac2}{A^2c3 + A + c4} + c5\sin(Ac6+c7)\)
Kill linear: \(c1=0\). Kill rational: \(c2=0\). Then match with \(c0=-0.5637...\), \(c5=0.131378...\), \(c6=0.761691...\), \(c7=0\). **Match possible.**

### 51. \(Ac0 + Ac1 + Ac2 e^{c3 t} + c4e^{Ac5} + c6\sin(Ac7+c8)\)
No \(A^2\) term; cannot match. **No match.**

### 52. \(Ac0 + A^{c1}c2 + c3e^{Ac4} + c5\sin(Ac6+c7)\)
Kill linear: \(c0=0\). Kill exp: \(c3=0\). Set \(c1=2\), \(c2=-0.5637...\), and sine params. **Match possible.**

### 53. \(Ac0 + c1e^{Ac2} + c3\log(c4 t+1) + c5\sin(Ac6+c7)\)
No \(A^2\) term; also explicit \(t\) in log. **No match.**

### 54. \(Ac0 + Ac1 + c2e^{Ac3} + c4\sin(Ac5+c6)\)
No \(A^2\) term. **No match.**

### 55. \(A^{c0}c1 + A^{c2}c3 + c4 e^{Ac5}\sin(Ac6+c7)\)
To match GT need sine amplitude constant, so require \(c5=0\) making \(e^{Ac5}=1\). Then sine term ok. For polynomial part, set one power to quadratic and kill the other: \(c0=2\), \(c1=-0.5637...\), \(c3=0\). Sine: \(c4=0.131378...\), \(c6=0.761691...\), \(c7=0\). **Match possible.**

### 56. \(Ac0 e^{c1 t} + c2e^{Ac3} + c4\sin(Ac5+c6)\)
No \(A^2\) term; also \(t\) dependence unless \(c0=0\) or \(c1=0\). Still cannot create quadratic. **No match.**

### 57. \(Ac0 + c1e^{Ac2} + c3e^{c4 t} + c5\sin(Ac6+c7)\)
No \(A^2\) term; also \(t\) term. **No match.**

### 58. \(Ac0 + Ac1 + Ac2 t + c3e^{Ac4} + c5\sin(Ac6+c7)\)
No \(A^2\) term; explicit \(t\) unless \(c2=0\). Still no quadratic. **No match.**

### 59. \(Ac0 + c1e^{Ac2} + c3\sin(c4 t+c5) + c6\sin(Ac7+c8)\)
No \(A^2\) term; also \(t\)-sine. **No match.**

### 60. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + c2\sin(Ac3+c4) + c5e^{Ac6} + c7\)
Kill linear: \(c1=0\). Kill exp: \(c5=0\). Kill constant: \(c7=0\). Then match with \(c0=-0.5637...\), sine params as usual. **Match possible.**

### 61. \(Ac0 + Ac1 + Ac2\sin(c3+c4 t) + c5e^{Ac6} + c7\sin(Ac8+c9)\)
No \(A^2\) term. Also \(t\)-dependent sine unless \(c2=0\). Still cannot match. **No match.**

### 62. \(Ac0 + c1e^{Ac2} + c3\sin(Ac4+c5)\)
No \(A^2\) term. **No match.**

### 63. \(c0e^{Ac1} + c2 e^{c3 e^{Ac4}} + \frac{c5 t}{c6 t+c7} + \frac{c8}{c6 t+c7}\)
No sine or quadratic; heavy \(t\) dependence. **No match.**

### 64. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + \frac{Ac2}{A^2c3 + A + c4} + A^{c5}c6 e^{Ac7} e^{c8 t}\)
Need no \(t\): set \(c6=0\) (or \(c8=0\) and also handle \(e^{Ac7}\), but easiest \(c6=0\)). Then same as candidate 50 without sine term; but candidate 64 then has no sine at all. If instead keep last term to act as sine: impossible since it’s power*exponential, not sine. So must rely on other terms—none are sine. **No match.**

### 65. \(Ac0 + Ac1e^{c2 t} + c3e^{Ac4} + c5\sin(Ac6+c7)\)
No \(A^2\) term. **No match.**

### 66. \(Ac0 + c1e^{Ac2} + c3\sin(Ac4+c5) + c6\sin(Ac7+c8)\)
No \(A^2\) term. **No match.**

### 67. \(Ac0 + Ac1 t + c2e^{Ac3} + c4\sin(Ac5+c6)\)
No \(A^2\) term; also explicit \(t\). **No match.**
